SHES BYA'I GTER MDZOD,...

SI KHRON MI RIGS DPE SKRUN KHANG,

*, ,BOD GANGS CAN GYI GRUB MTHA' RIS MED KYI MKHAS DBANG BRGYA
DANG BRGYAD CU LHAG GI GSUNG 'BUM SO SO'I DKAR CHAG PHYOGS GCIG
TU BSGRIGS PA SHES BYA'I GTER MDZOD CES BYA BA BZHUGS SO, ,

(STOD CHA)

MI RIGS DPE MDZOD KHANG GIS BSGRIGS PA,

SI KHRON MI RIGS DPE SKRUN KHANG,

@01

GLENG GZHI,

BOD RIGS NI RANG RGYAL GYI LO RGYUS YUN RING LDAN PA'I MI RIGS
RLABS CHEN ZHIG YIN LA, LAS LA BRTZON ZHING DPA' BA DANG, BLO
RIG LDAN PA ZHIG KYANG RED, RLABS CHEN GYI MES RGYAL GSAR GTOD
BYED PA'I GO RIM NANG DU BYAS RJES 'OD STONG 'BAR BA BZHAG YOD
CING, LO RGYUS 'PHEL RGYAS KYI CHU KLUNG RING PO 'DI'I NANG DU
BOD KYI MI RIGS DANG MI RIGS GZHAN DAG THUN MONG THOG NAS MES
RGYAL GYI RIG GZHUNG 'OD STONG RAB TU 'PHRO BA ZHIG GSAR GTOD
BYAS YOD PA RED, BOD YIG GI DPE RNYING 'DI DAG NI MES RGYAL MI
RIGS KYI RIG GZHUNG GI NOR MDZOD NANG GI MU TIG GZI 'OD RAB TU
'PHRO BA ZHIG RED,

BOD YIG GI DPE RNYING DE DAG DUS RABS BCU GCIG PA'I GONG LA
SANGS RGYAS KYI GSUNG RAB BSGYUR RGYU DE GTZO BOR BYAS SHING, DE
NI BOD KYI BTZAN PO MES DBON RNAM GSUM GYI DUS NAS 'GO TSUGS PA
ZHIG RED, BTZAN PO KHRI SRONG LDE BTZAN GYI SKABS SU BSGYUR ZIN
PA'I GSUNG RAB THAMS CAD DKAR CHAG TU BKOD PA 'PHANG THANG MA
DANG, MCHIMS PHU MA, LDAN DKAR MA GSUM YOD RUNG 'PHANG MCHIMS
GNYIS KYI DKAR CHAG 'THOR GYAR DU SONG BAS LDAN DKAR MA TZAM LAS
MA SUS PA DE NI BSTAN 'GYUR GYI SNA TSOGS ZHES PA'I KHROD DU
BZHUGS PA 'DI YIN, DKAR CHAG 'DI'I NANG BKA' BSTAN GNYIS SDE
TSAN BCU DGUR PHYES TE THEG CHEN DANG, THEG DMAN, MDO PHYOGS,
SNGAGS PHYOGS, SDE SNOD GSUM BCAS KYI GO RIM LTAR PHYE THOG  MDO
SDE'I SDE SNOD NANG PHAR PHYIN DANG, PHAL CHEN, DKON BRTZEGS,
BSDUS PA CHEN PO BCAS KYI GO RIM LTAR BSGRIGS 'DUG  DE NI GSUNG
RAB SDE TSAN DBYE BA'I SROL THOG MAR GTOD PA ZHIG RED,

BOD LA SANGS RGYAS CHOS LUGS DAR BA DANG CHABS CIG CHOS LUGS
GRUB MTHA' 'DRA MIN 'GA' RE BYUNG BA'I 'GO TSUGS SHING, DUS RABS
BCU GCIG PA TSUN TZAM LA GSUNG RAB DE DAG GI DGONGS 'GREL DANG,
LO RGYUS, SKAD YIG  RIG GNAS SKOR SOGS KYI RTZOM

@02

RIGS JE MANG DU PHYIN TE RTZOM RIGS KYI GLEGS BAM HA CANG MANG
PO ZHIG DAR PA RED, DA DAG NI BOD YIG GI DPE RNYING NANG GI GRUB
CHA GAL CHEN ZHIG RED, NANG DON MDOR BSDUS NA RIG GNAS CHE BA
LNGA STE BZO RIG PA DANG, GSO BA RIG PA, SGRA RIG PA, GTAN TSIGS
RIG PA, NANG DON RIG PA BCAS DANG, RIG GNAS CHUNG BA LNGA STE
SNYAN NGAG DANG, MNGON BRJOD, SDEB SBYOR, ZLOS GAR, SKAR RTZIS
BCAS YOD PA RED, LHAG PAR DU LO RGYUS DANG RNAM THAR SKOR GYI
RTZOM RIGS MANG TZAM ZHIG YOD PA DE'I NANG NAS BSTAN RTZIS RE'U
MIG DANG, RGYAL RABS, MI RIGS BAR GYI 'BREL BA'I SKOR GYI LO
RGYUS, CHOS 'BYUNG, GRUB MTHA' SO SO'I BLA RGYUD, GDUNG RABS,
RANG RNAM, GSANG BA'I RNAM THAR SOGS DANG, GNAS YIG DANG, DGON
PA'I GDAN RABS SOGS YOD PAR MA ZAD, GZHAN YANG MGUR MA DANG,
LEGS BSHAD, TSIG SPEL MA'I SNYAN NGAG GI GTAM RGYUD SOGS KYANG
YOD LA, GNA' DUS RGYA GAR GYI SKAD YIG SAm SKRi TA'I SGRA RIG PA
DANG, GTAN TSIGS RIG PA, SNYAN NGAG SOGS GSAL BSHAD BYED PA'I
MCHAN 'GREL SKOR GYI RTZOM RIGS KYANG MI NYUNG BA ZHIG YOD PA
RED, DE DAG KHYON YONGS KYI GRANGS 'BOR JI TZAM YOD PA NI RE RE
BZHIN BRJOD KYIS MI LANG NGO, GONG GSAL RIG GNAS SHUL BZHAG 'DI
DAG NI BOD KYI SANGS RGYAS CHOS LUGS DANG BOD RIGS KYI RIG
GZHUNG LA BRTAG DPYAD BYED RGYUR BLANGS NA RDZOGS RGYU MED PA
DANG SPYAD NA 'DZAD MTHA' MED PA'I BANG MDZOD CIG YIN PAS RANG
CAG GIS BRTZI MTHONG CHEN PO BYED 'OS PA ZHIG RED,

GSUNG 'BUM SKOR GYI RTZOM RIGS NI BKA' BSTAN 'GYUR GYI KHONGS
SU MA GTOGS PA'I DPE RNYING RTZOM RIGS KYI GRUB CHA GTZO BO ZHIG
YIN LA BOD YIG DPE RNYING GI BCUD LTA BU RED, DUS RABS BCO
BRGYAD PA'I MJUG LA KLONG RDOL BLA MA NGAG DBANG BLO BZANG GIS
<BKA' GDAMS PA DANG DGE LUGS PA'I BLA MA RAGS RIM GYI GSUNG 'BUM
MTSAN THO> BSGRIGS PA DE'I NANG LA GSUNG 'BUM KHAG BZHI BCU TZAM
LAS, BU STON RIN CHEN GRUB DANG, RJE TZONG KHA PA SOGS MKHAS
DBANG KHA SHAS KYI GSUNG 'BUM LE TSAN DPE THO ZHIB PHRA TZAM
DANG, DE MIN MDOR BSDUS SHIG BKOD 'DUG CING, DUS RABS BCU DGU
PA'I DKYIL LA DRUNG CHEN SHES RAB RGYA MTSOS <DPE RGYUN DKON PA
'GA' ZHIG GI THO YIG DON GNYER YID KYI KUN D'A BZHAD PA'I

@03

ZLA 'OD 'BUM GYI SNYE MA> ZHES PA BSGRIGS PA DE'I NANG DU SDE
TSAN BCU GNYIS SU PHYES TE GSUNG 'BUM KHAG DGU BCU'I MTSAN THO
BKOD 'DUG 1959 LOR BLA BRANG BKRA SHIS 'KHYIL DU SNUM PAR THOG
DKOD PA'I <BLA BRANG DGON PA'I DPE CHA SPYI'I DKAR CHAG> NANG LA
SDE KHAG CHE BA BCU BDUN BGOS SHING, GSUNG 'BUM SKOR LA MKHAS
DBANG 174 YI DPE THO BKOD 'DUG

BOD RIGS KYI RIG GNAS BYA GZHAG SHUL 'DZIN DANG DAR SPEL BYED
RGYU DANG, MI RIGS KHAG GI RIG GNAS BRJE RES BYED RGYU, THUN
MONG DU DAR RGYAS PHUN SUM TSOGS PA YONG BAR SKUL SPEL GTONG
RGYU, MI RIGS KYI TSAN RIGS ZHIB 'JUG GI BYA BA BYED RGYU, DNGOS
PO DANG BSAM BLO'I DPAL YON GNYIS KYI 'DZUGS SKRUN BYED RGYU
BCAS LA ZHABS 'DEGS ZHU BA'I CHED DU 'DI GA DPE MDZOD KHANG GI
BOD YIG DPE RNYING LEGS SGRI BYED PAI RMANG BZHI'I THOG 'DI GAR
BZHUGS YOD PA'I BOD YIG DPE RNYING NANG GSUNG 'BUM SKOR GYI DKAR
CHAG ZHIB PHRA BSGRIGS NAS, THOG MAR DEB 'DI BSGRIGS PA YIN, DEB
'DI'I NANG KHYON BSDOMS MKHAS DBANG BRGYA DANG BRGYAD CU RTZAM
GYI GSUNG 'BUM 'DUS YOD CING, DEB GSUM DU BGOS TE RIM PAS PAR
BSKRUN BYED RGYU YIN, GSUNG 'BUM SKOR GYI DKAR CHAG 'DI NI DPE
CHA DANG DPYAD GZHI SOGS 'TSOL BDE CHED BOD RGYA SKAD GNYIS SHAN
SBYAR BYAS NAS BKOD YOD PA'I LAG CHA LTA BU'I DEB CIG YIN, 'ON
KYANG 'DI GA'I DPE MDZOD KHANG DU YOD PA'I DPE CHA'I GNAS TSUL
MTSON PA TZAM ZHIG LAS, BOD YIG DPE RNYING NANG GSUNG 'BUM SKOR
GYI RTZOM RIGS YOD DO COG GI RNAM PA YONGS SU MTSON MI THUB,

BOD YIG DPE RNYING RNAMS LA DPE MING RGYAS PA DANG BSDUS PA
GNYIS YOD CING, DPE MING RGYAS PA DE DAG HA CANG RING BAS BLOR
NGES DKA' BA DANG, LHAG PAR DU THUN MONG MA YIN PA'I KHYAD CHOS
DMIGS BSAL RE YOD LA, THA SNYAD DANG MNGON BRJOD RNAM GRANGS
MANG BAS KLOG PA POS GO DKA' BA ZHIG DANG, DPE MING KHA BYANG
BSDUS PA DE DAG NI MING 'DRA BA MANG BAS DKAR CHAG BZO DUS RNYOG
'DZING YONG SLA BA ZHIG RED, DER BRTEN DPE CHA'I KHA BYANG YONGS
RDZOGS JI BZHIN BSHUS NAS DKAR CHAG BZOS YOD,

NGA TSOS CHED DMIGS KYIS RTZOM PA PO SO SO'I GNAS TSUL MDOR
BSDUS RE NGO SPROD ZHUS YOD, DE'I NANG RTZOM PA PO 'GA' ZHIG GI
RNAM THAR SOGS DPYAD GZHI 'DZOM PO ZHIG MA RNYED

@04

STABS GSAN YIG DANG, MJUG BYANG, BLA BRGYUD SOGS 'BREL YOD DPYAD
GZHIR BRTEN NAS NGO SPRAD BYAS YOD, RTZOM PA PO 'GA' ZHIG LA
DPYAD GZHI MA RNYED STABS BAR STONG LA 'JOG DGOS BYUNG,

DKAR CHAG 'DI BZO BA'I GO RIM NANG LA PE CIN DPE MDZOD KHANG
DANG, KRUNG DBYANG MI RIGS SKAD YIG YIG SGYUR CUS, MI RIGS DPE
SKRUN KHANG, KRUNG DBYANG MI RIGS SLOB GRVA CHEN MO, MTSO SNGON
MI RIGS SLOB GRVA CHEN MO, BOD LJONGS MI RIGS SLOB GRVA CHEN MO,
SI KHRON MI RIGS DPE SKRUN KHANG SOGS 'BREL YOD LAS KHUNGS KHAG
NAS RGYAB SKYOR SHUGS CHEN GNANG BAR SNYING THAG PA NAS THUGS
RJE CHE ZHU RGYU YIN,

NGA TSOS BOD RYA SHAN SBYAR GYI DKAR CHAG CHE GRAS 'DI 'DRA ZHIG
BSGRIGS PA THENGS DANG PO YIN PAS NYAMS MYONG MI 'DANG BA DANG,
MI SHUGS MI 'DANG BA, BOD KYI RIG GNAS KHYAB KHONGS KYI YON TSAD
DMA' BA BCAS LA BRTEN SKYON DANG NOR 'KHRUL YOD NGES LA MKHAS
DBANG RNAM PA DANG, KLOG PA PO RNAMS KYIS MDZUB STON GNANG BA'I
RE 'DUN ZHU RGYU BCAS,

@01

DKAR CHAG SGRIG TSUL SKOR GYI GSAL BSHAD,

1 DKAR CHAG 'DI NI GSUNG 'BUM GYI RTZOM PA PO SO SO'I MTSAN
ZUR LAS DRAS PA'I KA KHA'I GO RIM LTAR BSGRIGS YOD, GRUB
MTHA'I BLA BRGYUD DANG SKU RABS GRAGS CHE BA RNAMS DE'I GO RIM
JI BZHIN MTSON PAR BYED CHED, SPYI MING BKOD YOD PA DPER NA
KARMA PA SKU PHRENG RIM BYON GYI GSUNG 'BUM LA ``KA YIG''
DANG, T'A LA'I SKU PHRENG RIM BYON GYI GSUNG 'BUM LA ``T'A
YIG'' SA SKYA'I GONG MA LNGA'I GSUNG 'BUM LA ``SA YIG'' BCAS
GZHIR BZHAG NAS KA MAD RIM PA LTAR BSGRIGS SHING, BLA BRGYUD
DANG SKU RABS SO SO'I NANG KHUL GYI RTZOM PA PO'I MTSAN NI SKU
PHRENG SNGA PHYI'I GO RIM LTAR BSGRIGS YOD,

2 GSUNG 'BUM TSAR RER PAR MA'AM BRIS MA GANG RUNG ZHIG LA CHA
BZHAG NAS, SNGON GYI GLEGS BAM DANG DPE TSAN BSGRIGS TSUL SOR
BZHAG THOG PAR GZHI GZHAN LA'ANG ZUR BLTAS BYAS TE, MA TSANG
BA RNAMS KHA SKONG BYAS YOD, DPER NA DNGUL CHU DBYANGS CAN
GRUB PA'I RDO RJE'I GSUNG 'BUM GA POD NANG AANG GRANGS 004524
RTAGS CAN RNAMS NI PAR GZHI GZHAN NAS DRANGS PA'I RTAGS YIN,
'GA' ZHIG NI LOGS SU BSGRIGS YOD,

3 PAR GZHI MI 'DRA BA'I NANG LA NANG DON 'DRA YANG KHA BYANG
MI 'DRA BA YOD PA DPER NA TZONG KHA PA'I GSUNG 'BUM KHA POD
NANG LA LHA SA'I PAR MAR LAM RIM LA <SKYES BU GSUM GYI NYAMS
SU BLANGS PA'I BYANG CHUB LAM GYI RIM PA BZHUGS SO> ZHES 'KHOD
PA DANG, SDE DGE'I PAR MAR <RGYAL BA'I GSUNG RAB THAMS CAD KYI
SNYING PO'I GNAD BSDUS TE GTAN LA PHAB PA BYANG CHUB LAM GYI
RIM PA BZHUGS SO> ZER BA LTA BU KHA BYANG MI 'DRA BA RNAMS SO
SOR BKOD YOD, NANG DON MI 'DRA YANG KHA BYANG MTSUNGS PA DPER
NA <KUN MKHYEN CHOS KYI RGYAL PO RIG 'DZIN 'JIGS MED GLING
PA'I BKA' 'BUM YONGS RDZOGS KYI BZHUGS BYANG CHOS RAB RNAM
'BYED CES BYA BA BZHUGS,> 000541 RTAGS CAN NANG GI (38) (39)
PAR GSAL BA DE

@02

RIGS KYANG SO SOR BKOD YOD,

NANG DON 'DRA LA KHA BYANG YANG DE TZAM DBYE BA CHER MED PAS
DBYE 'BYED SLA TZAM YOD PA RNAMS GCIG GIS 'THUS PA BYAS YOD,

4 PO TI SO SO'I GDONG TSAL LA YOD PA'I AANG GRANGS DANG KHA
BSKONG DU DRANGS PA'I DPE TSAN SO SO'I GSHAM LA YOD PA'I AANG
GRANGS NI RANG RE'I DPE MDZOD KHANG GI POD GRANGS MTSON BYED
YIN, DPE TSAN GSHAM GYI( )RTAGS YOD PA 'DI NI PO TI DE'I NANG
GI DPE TSAN GYI GO RIM MTSON PA'I AANG GRANGS YIN,( )RTAGS KYI
RGYAB LA YOD PA'I AANG KI DE NI SHOG GRANGS MTSON BYED YIN,

@02

'OD KYI PHRENG BA BZHUGS, ,...(2) 270

RTZOM PA PO'I LO RGYUS NYUNG BSDUS,...

* ,KARMA PA SKU PHRENG GSUM PA RANG BYUNG RDO RJE NI, GTZANG
STOD SKYID GRONG 'PHAGS PA WA

TI'I LHA KHANG GI LHO PHYOGS GANGS ZHUR MO ZHES PAR YAB CHOS
DPAL DANG, YUM JO MO G-YANG 'DREN

GNYIS KYI SRAS SU RAB BYUNG LNGA PA'I SHING PHO SPREL LOR (1284)
'KHRUNGS, DGUNG LO LNGA PAR GRUB CHEN

AO RGYAN PA RIN CHEN DPAL MJAL BAR BYON, GRUB CHEN PAS, NGA'I
BLA MA'I GSANG MTSAN RANG BYUNG

RDO RJE YIN PAS DE KA 'DOGS GSUNGS NAS RANG BYUNG RDO RJER MTSAN
GSOL, DGE BSNYEN GYI SDOM

PA DANG SEMS BSKYED GNANG, DGUNG LO BDUN PAR KHRO PHU SHES RAB
KYIS MKHAS PO MDZAD DE DGE TSUL

BSGRUBS, 'DUL BA GSAN, RTA LOR SA G-YOS BYUNG BA'I SHING RTA
LO'I (1294) RJES KYI LO SHAS

DE'I NANG LA GNAS BRTAN GZHON NU 'BYUNG BAS MKHAN PO DANG, DGE
'DUN RIN CHEN GYIS LAS SLOB

MDZAD DE BSNYEN PAR RDZOGS, 'DUL BA YONGS RDZOGS GSAN, SLOB DPON
SHES RAB DPAL, RGYA

SGOM YE SHES, SNYE MDO KUN DGA' DON GRUB SOGS LAS BOD KYI YUL DU
BKA' BSTAN 'GYUR RO 'TSAL

THAMS CAD GSAN PAR MDZAD, DE NAS KARMA'I GDAN SAR BYON, SA SKYA
'JAM DBYANGS RIN CHEN

RGYAL MTSAN DER PHEBS PA DANG MJAL NAS GSUNG GLENG MDZAD, KHA BA
DKAR POR BYON NAS GNAS YIG

BRTZAMS, DE NAS KAM PO GNAS NANG DU BYON, CHU GLANG LOR (1313)
TZ'A RIR PHEBS, ZLA BA GSUM

BZHUGS, MTSUR PHUR TSUR PHEBS, SHING BYA LOR (1325) KONG POR
GDAN DRANGS, DER SGRUB

SDE 'GA' ZHIG BTAB, MDO KHAMS SU BYON, SOG CHUR LCAGS ZAM
BTZUGS, DE NAS HOR

RGYAL POS GDAN 'DREN BYAS, LCAGS LUG LOR (1331) GSER YIG PA MGON
PO TSIM CHING SOGS

DBUS SU SLEBS PAS CHOS RJE KONG PO NAS GDAN DRANGS, GDAN ZHU'I
'JA' SA BSGRAGS, SA SKYA'I TI SHR'I

KUN DGA' RGYAL MTSAN NAS MES RGYAL NANG KHUL DU PHEBS DGOS TSUL
ZHUS, KUN RGYAN PA RANG NYID SNGON

DU PHEBS, CHU SPREL LO'I (1332) ZLA GNYIS PA'I TSES GCIG LA STOD
LUNG MTSUR PHU NAS BTEG ZLA BA

BRGYAD PA'I TSES BCU GNYIS LA RGYAL PO GSHEGS NAS MJAL MA THUB
KYANG, CHU SPREL ZLA BCU GCIG PA'I

TSES BCO BRGYAD LA PHO BRANG CHEN POR 'BYOR, RGYAL BU RAT NA
SHRI SOGS KYIS BSU BA RGYA CHEN PO BYAS, DE

RJES RGYAL BU YANG 'DAS, DE'I GCEN PO THO GAN THE MUR SMAN
RTZE'I YUL NAS GDAN DRANGS, DE NAS RGYAL

PO THO GAN THE MUR DANG BTZUN MO BLON PO SOGS LA DBANG BSKUR
CHOS BSHAD GNANG, DE NAS SHING KHYI'I

LOR (1334) CHOS RJE BOD DU PHEBS KHAR TSAL PA SI TU DGE SBYONG

MDO'I NUB BYANG NGOS KYI NGOM CHU RGYUD

G-YAS LUNG KAR TI PHUG PA TAM ZER BAR YAB AA BYAMS DANG, YUM
BLA MA SGRON GNYIS KYI SRAS SU

RAB BYUNG DGU PA'I ME YOS LOR (1507) SKU 'KHRUNGS, ZLA NGO BDUN
BZHES PA NA RI BO CHER BYON,

BSNYEN BKUR CHER ZHUS, DE NAS LHO RONG RDZONG DU SPYAN DRANGS PA
LTAR BYON, DGUNG LO LNGA TZAM LA

PHEBS DUS, RGYAL TSAB BKRA SHIS RNAM RGYAL DANG RI BO CHE'I MI
SNA LHO RONG GI GO SHRI SOGS NAS KARMA

PA'I SKU PHRENG YIN PAR THAG BCAD, DE NAS CHU BYA LOR (1513)
KHRI 'DON BYAS, RGYAL TSAB RIN

PO CHE BKRA SHIS RNAM RGYAL ('DI MTSUR PHU RGYAL TSAB SPRUL SKU
ZER BA'I SKU THOG DANG PO DE YIN,) LAS THEG

CHEN SO THAR GYI SDOM PA BZHES TE MTSAN CHOS KYI GRAGS PA DPAL
BZANG POR GSOL, YI GE 'BRI

KLOG LA BRTZON PAR MDZAD, DE NAS MDO KHAMS SHAR PHYOGS SU BYON,
DGUNG LO BRGYAD PA LA ZUR

MANG (MTSO SNGON LHO RGYUD SKYE RGU MDO'I LHO NUB DANG NYE BAR
ZUR MANG CHE CHUNG GNYIS YOD PA DE'O,) DU BYON,

DE NAS 'DAN MA GRUB CHEN SANGS RGYAS MNYAN RAS NAS BYANG CHUB
GLING DU GDAN DRANGS, ZHVA KHRA CAN STONG

PHRAG LHAG GIS BSU BA BYAS, DE NAS KAM PO GANGS RAR (KAM PO GNAS
NANG) PHEBS SHING,

'JANG SA THAM RGYAL POS GDAN 'DREN BYUNG BAS RIM PAR BYON, ME
BYI LOR (1516) SA THAM DU PHEBS,

@16

BSU BA LA RGYAL PO NYID GYAM KHRIR PHEBS, KHU BO DANG NU BO
GNYIS GLANG CHEN ZHON, GLANG CHEN GCIG

YAN PAR KHRID, RTA PA MANG POS GDUGS DANG RGYAL MTSAN THOGS NAS
BSU BA BYA, PHO BRANG DU SPYAN

DRANGS TE BKUR BZOS BLA LHAG TU BYAS, SA THAM RGYAL POS BOD LA
LO BCU GSUM BAR DMAG KHRAL

DANG BU KHRAL (BTZUN KHRAL) LO LTAR LNGA BRGYA RE PHUL, DGON PA
BRGYA 'DEBS PAR KHAS BLANGS, [ME

BYI 'DI NAS BRTZIS PA'I LO RE BZHI TZAM SONG PA'I LOR (1580) T'A
LA'I GSUM PA BSOD NAMS RGYA

MTSOS LI THANG DU LI THANG THEG CHEN CHOS 'KHOR GLING BTAB, DE
DUS SBYIN BDAG SA THAM RGYAL POS BYAS

PA'I LO RGYUS BEE SER DANG LI THANG DGON PAR T'A LA'I BDUN PAS
BSTZAL PA'I BKA' SHOG DANG BCA' YIG

NANG 'KHOD PA NGO MA ZHIG DNGOS SU MTHONG BAS ZUR 'DEBS KYI TSUL
DU BRIS SO,] SA THAM DU ZHAG

BDUN BZHUGS, LO BDUN MTSAMS NAS 'BYON PAR ZHAL BZHES GNANG,
SKYEL MA DANG BCAS TSUR

BYON, SA THAM RGYAL POS RGYAL TSAB GSHEGS PA'I DGONGS RDZOGS SU
DGE 'DUN PAR GSER ZHO RE 'GYED

DANG, GDUNG RTEN BZHENGS RGYUR GSER ZHO LNGA BRGYA, ZANGS DOS
BCU, THUB CHEN GSER THOG

RGYUR ZANGS DOS SUM CU, GSER ZHO LTONG RVA CAN, JA BRGYA SOGS
GNANG, DE NAS DKAR MDZES

KHUL GYI NYAG CHU GRU KHA SOGS BRGYUD NAS PHEBS, 'DAN MA GRUB
CHEN SANGS RGYAS MNYAN RAS KYI MDUN

NAS DGUNG LO BCU PAR DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA BZHES, CHOS BKA' DBANG
LUNG CI RIGS GSAN,

DE NAS 'DAN KHOG BYANG CHUB GLING DU BYON, SANGS RGYAS MNYAN PAS
SGAR PA STONG PHRAG GI PHOG PHUL,

DER LO GSUM TZAM BZHUGS NAS DBANG LUNG KHRID GSUM GSAN, SA YOS
(1519) TZAM LA RGYA NAG TU

PHEBS DGOS PA'I GSER YIG PA 'BYOR YANG MA PHEBS, DE NAS KONG POR
BYON, KONG PO

BU CHUR RGYAL TSAB SPRUL SKU'I GTZUG PHUD BZHES, MTSAN GRAGS PA
DPAL 'BYOR ZHES PA GNANG, MON

RGYAL POS GSER LJANG RDUNG GI PAD ZHU PHUL, DGUNG LO NYER GCIG
PAR MKHAN CHEN CHOS GRUB SENG GE

DANG SLOB DPON KARMA 'PHRIN LAS PA SOGS LAS BSNYEN PAR RDZOGS,
MKHAN SLOB GNYIS KYI MDUN NAS

BKA' CHOS MANG DU GSAN, KARMA LO TZ'A BA RIN CHEN BKRA SHIS LAS
SGRA DANG SUM RTAGS SOGS GSAN,

DE DUS SKABS SHIG LA PHRAG YUL SOGS YON MCHOD THAMS CAD GROS
MTHUN GYIS KONG PO KHUL GYI DGE

LUGS DGON SDE BRLAG PAR BRTZAM PA NA, CHOS RJES BKAG PAR MDZAD,
DE LTAR KHAMS KONG KHUL RGYUN

RING TZAM BZHUGS NAS DGUNG LO SO GCIG PAR MTSUR PHUR BYON, DE
DUS DBUS GTZANG GI BAR CHINGS

MDZAD, SKU TSE'I MJUG TU TZ'A RIR GNAS SKOR PHEBS NAS DGUNG LO
ZHE BRGYAD BZHES PA'I SHING STAG LO'I

ZHES PA'I YUL DU RAB BYUNG BCU BZHI PA'I SA MO BYA'I LO (1849)
LA 'KHRUNGS, SKU BLTAMS NAS YUN

MI RING BAR YAB BDE CHEN NAS 'PHRIN LAS RDO RJE ZHES PA'I MTSAN
GSOL, DGUNG GRANGS LNGA PAR PHEBS

SKABS, 'JAM BZHAD SKU PHRENG GSUM PA 'JIGS MED RGYA MTSO MCHOG
NAS, RONG PO CHOS RJE'I SKU SKYE

RU NGOS 'DZIN MDZAD, BLO BZANG 'PHRIN LAS BSTAN PA RGYA MTSO
ZHES PA'I MTSAN BSTZAL, DGUNG LO DRUG

PA NAS AA LAGS BSTAN PA YONGS 'DZIN DU BSTEN, 'BRI KLOG SOGS
SLOB 'GO TSUGS, BLA BRANG BKRA

SHIS 'KHYIL GYI 'DU KHANG CHEN MOR KHRI STON MDZAD, DGE BSHES
THUB BSTAN MTHA' YAS LA MDO SNGAGS KYI

GZHUNG MANG PO GSAN PA DANG, RJE DKON MCHOG SMON LAM BZANG PO'I
MDUN NAS RAB TU BYUNG,

DGUNG LO BRGYAD PAR DKON MCHOG SMON LAM MDUN DGE TSUL GYI SDOM
PA BZHES, DGUNG LO BCU GCIG

PA NAS NYER BZHI'I BAR YONGS 'DZIN DANG MTSAN ZHABS PA DGE BSHES
CHEN PO RNAMS KYI MDUN NAS

GZHUNG POD LNGA LA SBYANGS PA MTHAR PHYIN MDZAD, DGUNG LO NYER
BZHI PAR RANG GI GDAN SAR RJE BTZUN

NGAG DBANG CHOS 'PHEL MDUN BSNYEN RDZOGS KYI SDOM PA BZHES, RAB
BYUNG BCO LNGA PA'I CHU MO BYA'I LOR

SI KHRON RNGA PA'I YUL DU DGON GSAR PHAL CHER BTAB GRUB CING
DGON DE'I GDAN SAR BZHUGS TE,

BSHAD GRVA DANG SGRUB GRVA BTZUGS TE BSTAN PA RGYA CHER SPEL,
DGUNG LO NGA DRUG TU PHEBS PA RAB BYUNG

BCO LNGA PA'I SHING MO SBRUL GYI LO (1905) LA RANG DGON DU SKU
GSHEGGS SO,

KHONG NI DBUS GTZANG DU PHEBS MA MYONG YANG, MDO SMAD KYI DGON
SDE PHAL MO CHE DANG, SOG YUL

GYI DGON SDE 'GAR ZHABS KYIS BCAGS TE, SKU TSE HRIL POR RTEN
GSAR BZHENGS DANG 'CHAD NYAN GYIS

DUS 'DA' BAR MDZAD CING, GZHUNG LUGS RGYA MTSOR 'BAD PA LHUR LEN
MDZAD DE MKHAS PAR GYUR,

*, SA SKYA BLA MA BSOD NAMS LHUN GRUB LEGS PA'I 'BYUNG GNAS
NI, RAB BYUNG BDUN PA'I

LCAGS MO BYA'I LO (1441) LA 'KHRUNGS SHING, KHONG NI SA KYA
DRUNG CHEN PA LA SRAS SPUN MCHED BZHI

YOD PA'I NANG, SPUN THA CHUNG YIN, SKU MCHED GSUM POS SRID
SKYONG BA'I BYA BA MDZAD CING,

KHONG CHOS LAM DU ZHUGS TE, DGUNG LO GNYIS PAR YUM DANG LHAN
CIG 'JAM DBYANGS SHES RAB

RGYA MTSO'I MDUN NAS SKYABS 'GRO'I SDOM PA DANG, GTZUG GTOR
RNAM PAR RGYAL BA'I RJES GNANG SOGS

ZHAG BDUN GYI RING LA ZHUS, DGUNG LO GSUM PA'I DUS SU BSOD
NAMS RGYAL MTSAN DRUNG DU TSE DBANG

ZHUS, DGUNG LO LNGA DRUG GI DUS SU RNYING MA BA DGE LEGS RGYAL
MTSAN DRUNG DU, TSE DBANG DANG,

GU RU BKA' BRGYAD KYI DBANG SOGS DBANG MANG DU ZHUS, DGUNG LO
DGU PAR YON TAN CHOS RGYAL GYI

@90

DRUNG DU DGE BSNYEN GYI SDOM PA BLANGS, DGUNG LO BCU GNYIS PAR
RJE BTZUN KUN DGA' DBANG PHYUG

MDUN NAS DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA MNOS, RJE BTZUN KUN DGA' DBANG
PHYUG GIS, CHOS RJE RA CHEN

KYI SRAS SU, RAB BYUNG BCU GSUM PA'I CHU PHO RTA'I LO (1762) LA
'KHRUNGS, DGUNG LO BDUN PAR

KHRI CHEN DGE 'DUN PHUN TSOGS KYI SKYE PHRENG DU NGOS 'DZIN NAS
BLA BRANG BKRA SHIS 'KHYIL DU GDAN DRANGS,

'JAM DBYANGS BZHAD PAS DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA GNANG, MTSAN DKON
MCHOG BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME

BSTZAL, RDO RAMS PA BLO BZANG RIN CHEN KLOG GI SLOB DPON DU
BSTEN, 'BRI KLOG SBYOR SDEB

RAMS PA'I MTSAN BTAGS BZHES,

YONGS SU MKHAS PA'I GRAGS PAS KHYAB,

'JAM DBYANGS BZHAD PA'I ZHAL BSGOS LTAR BLA BRANG DU PHYIR
PHEBS, DGUNG LO SO GCIG PAR BLA BRANG

CHOS GRVA CHEN PO YONGS LA MKHAS TSUL

LO 'GA' BZHUGS TE,

NA'I BAR POD BCU GNYIS 'KHOD

MA MCHIS, KHONG GI GSUNG

NI MDO SNGAGS KYI GZHUNG TZAM MA ZAD, SGRA DANG BZO, SNYAN NGAG
DANG SMAN RTZIS SOGS THUN MONG RIG

GNAS SKOR PHUN SUM TSOGS PA'I BSTAN BCOS HA CANG MANG, DPER NA
CHU SHING GI BSTAN BCOS DANG,

*, DBYANGS CAN GRUB PA'I RDO RJE'AM, BLO BZANG CHOS 'PHEL GYI
'KHRUNGS YUL NI DBUS GTZANG

KHAMS GSUM LAS GTZANG G-YAS RU'I BYE BRAG BKRA SHIS DGE 'PHEL
GLING GI NYE 'DABS, SNGON DUS

'JAD CES GRAGS KYANG, RJES SU SLOB DPON PADMAS YUL DE'I CHE BA'I
DGE MTSAN LA ZHAL 'DZUM LAN

GSUM GROL BAS BZHAD CES PA'I MING THOB PA DER YIN LA, YAB DHARMA
BHA DRA'I GCUNG BKRA SHIS DANG

YUM TSE RING SRI CHOD GNYIS KYI SRAS SU RAB BYUNG BCU BZHI PA'I
SA MO SBRUL LO (1809) ZLA BA BCU PA'I

@406

TSES PA LNGA'I DGONG MOR SKU BLTAMS, DGUNG LO LNGA PAR KHU BO
DHARMA BHA DRA'I DRUNG DU KA KHA SBYONG BA'I

'GO BTZUGS, DE DUS BYIS PA'I MING 'JAM DBYANGS RDO RJE ZER, LO
GRANGS DRUG TZAM RING BLA

MA'I MDUN GSAN SBYONG BYAS PAS SBYOR SDEB BLO 'DZIN SOGS LA
THOGS PA MED PAR GYUR, DGUNG LO

BCU PAR BLA MA'I GZIM PHUG GI NYE 'GRAM RGYA MA BRAG PHUG CES
PAR THOB RGYAL BLA MA NGAG DBANG SNYAN

GRAGS MDUN GSAN SBYONG MDZAD PAR PHEBS, ZAS GOS SOGS KYI MTHUN
RKYEN TSANG MA KHU BO BLA MA NAS

SBYAR, RTZIS KYI SA RIS DANG SNYAN NGAG BCAS LA MKHO BA'I MNGON
BRJOD SNA TSOGS BLOR 'DZIN MDZAD,

SKABS DER YUM GYI MA HA CANG GCES PA'I RMOL RMOL ZHIG YOD PA
'DAS NAS, RANG KHYIM DU SKOR TZAM

PHEBS, DE 'PHRAL TSUR LOG STE GSAN SBYONG LA 'BAD, DGUNG LO BCU
GCIG PAR BKRA SHIS DGE

'PHEL DGON NAS GRVA KHRAL SDUD PAR BRTEN, KHONG YANG GRVA KHRAL
KHONGS NAS GRVA BTZUN MDZAD, DKA'

CHEN DKON MCHOG CHOS 'PHEL MDUN DU SKRA PHUD PHUL, MING BLO
BZANG CHOS 'PHEL BTAGS, DGUNG

LO BCU GNYIS PAR DKA' CHEN DKON MCHOG CHOS 'PHEL DRUNG NAS DGE
BSNYEN DANG DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA

MNOS, DE NAS BZUNG RJE MI LA'I RNAM MGUR DANG RO SGRUNG SOGS
DANG THIG TSAD DANG BLOS BSLANGS

BCAS MTHAR PHYIN PAR SBYANGS, DGUNG LO BCU BDUN PAR YAB TSONG LA
PHEBS PA JAG PAS BCOM

NAS BKRONGS, MA DANG NU MO BCAS RJES SU LUS KHONG MA SMAD SKYO
NGAL TSAD MED KYIS MNAR,

DGUNG LO NYI SHUR PHEBS PA NA, SHAR 'BROG NA MO CHE NAS BYANG
STA SGO'I BAR GYI 'BROG SDE RNAMS SU

DBYAR KHAR DGON PA'I DKAR SDUD LA SONG NAS ZLA BA GSUM TZAM
'GOR, DE NAS DGON PA'I TSOGS

SHING GNYER PA LO 'GAR MDZAD, MDOR NA DGON PAR DGUNG LO BCU GCIG
NAS BCU DGU'I BAR LO

BRGYAD RING 'DON RTA DBYANGS ROL MO SOGS NAS BLO 'DZIN DGOS RIGS
TSANG MA LEGS PAR GRUB CING,

DBANG LUNG SOGS KYANG MANG PO THOB BO, DGUNG LO BCU DGU PA NAS
BZUNG BLA MA DHARMA BHA DRA'I ZHABS

ZHU PA MDZAD DE SGRA DANG RTZIS, SNYAN NGAG DANG SUM RTAGS, MDO
DANG SNGAGS KYI GZHUNG CHEN MO

RNAMS SBYONG BA'I DBU TSUGS, DGUNG LO SO BZHI PAR BLA MA'I MDUN
SNYAN NGAG DANG SGRA KA LA PA'I RGYUd PHUL

BAS BLA MAS THUGS DGYES PA CHEN POS LEd SO DANG BCAS LHA RDZAS
SRID DU RING BA MGUL PAR BSTZAL TE,

MTSAN DBYANGS CAN GRUB PA'I RDO RJE ZHES PA GNANG, DE NAS BZUNG
MTSAN DE KUN BSHAD MING DU GYUR,

LO DE'I ZLA BA BZHI PA'I TSES BCO LNGA NYIN BLA MA CHOS BZANG
(DHARMA BHA DRA) DRUNG NAS DGE SLONG GI SDOM PA

MNOS, DE NAS BZUNG DGE SLONG GI BSLAB BYA'I 'KHRID SOGS 'DUL
BA'I SKOR GYI ZAB KHRID RGYA MTSO

LTA BU GSAN, BLA MA'I THUGS LA ZAB CHOS BZHUGS DGU BUM PA GANG
BYO'I TSUL GYIS ZHU ZHING RIG GNAS

CHE PHRA KUN LA MKHAS PA'I YANG RTZER SON, BLA MA'I GSUNG RTZOM
'GA'I YI GE PA'ANG KHONG GIS MDZAD,

DGUNG LO ZHE GSUM DU PHEBS PA RAB BYUNG BCU BZHI PA'I LCAGS MO
PHAG GI LO'I ZLA BA BZHI PA'I TSES

RTZOM PA PO'I LO RGYUS NYUNG BSDUS,...

*, RNGA RGOD NAM MKHA' SENG GE NI, MDO SMAD RNGOG PHYOGS KYI
SA YI CHAR GTOGS PA GSER BO

ZHES PA'I YUL DU, YAB MGON PO TSE RING DANG, YUM BAN DE MTSO
GNYIS KYI SRAS SU, RAB

BYUNG BCU GNYIS PA'I CHU PHO 'BRUG GI LO (1712) LA 'KHRUNGS,
DGUNG GRANGS LNGA PA'I DUS SU,

NGAR RGOD DPON GYIS BKAS BSKUL 'OG CHOS 'KHOR ZHABS DRUNG RIN
PO CHE NAS, RNGA RGOD BLA MA

DKA' BCU RDO RJE RGYAL MTSAN GYI SPRUL SKUR NGOS BZUNG, DGUNG
LO BDUN PAR 'BO RA NAS PHEBS  

PA'I BTZUN PA ZHIG DGE RGAN DU BSTEN NAS KLOG SLOB PA'I DBU
BTZUGS, 'DUL 'DZIN CHEN PO T'A

DPON SPRUL SKU'I MDUN DU RAB TU BYUNG ZHING DGE TSUL GYI SDOM
PA BLANGS, MTSAN NAM MKHA' SENG GE

ZHES GSOL, LO DE'I ZLA BA BCU PA'I TSES BCU'I NYIN PAR MDZAD
SGO'I RTEN 'BREL GZAB RGYAS DANG

BCAS BLA MA GONG MA'I GDAN KHRIR BZHUGS, KHU BO RAB 'BYAMS
SMRA BA BLO BZANG DPAL 'BYOR YONGS

'DZIN DU BSTEN NAS, RJE MI LA'I RNAM MGUR GYI KHRID LUNG DANG,
KUN RIG DANG 'JIGS BYED

SOGS KYI DBANG RJES GNANG BCAS MANG DU ZHUS PAR MA ZAD, DAM PA
DE NYID LA SMAN GYI RGYUD BZHI'I

LAG LEN SOGS GSAN CING, RGYUD KYI RTZA BA BLOR 'DZIN MDZAD,
RTZE DBUS PA BSOD NAMS RGYAL

MTSAN MDUN DU, DBYANGS CAN SGRA MDO'I RI MO SOGS SGRA'I SKOR

*, RNGA RGOD BLO BZANG BYAMS PA RAB RGYAS NI MDO SMAD KYI SA'I
CHAR SHIS TSANG ZHES PA'I YUL DU,

YAB GZUNGS 'BUM RGYAL DANG, YUM KLU MO GNYIS KYI SRAS SU, RAB
BYUNG BCU GSUM PA'I LCAGS

MO GLANG GI LO (1781) ZLA BA GNYIS PAR SKU BLTAMS, 'KHRUNGS MA
THAG TU, KHRI CHEN BLO BZANG

NYI MAS DKON MCHOG SKYABS ZHES PA'I MING BTAGS, DGUNG GRANGS
LNGA PAR 'JAM DBYANGS BZHAD PA

'JIGS MED DBANG POS RNGA RGOD NAM MKHA' SENG GE'I SKU SKYE RU
NGOS BZUNG, DGUNG LO DRUG PAR BKRA

SHIS 'KHYIL DU TSOGS CHEN KHRI PA RAB BRTAN RGYA MTSO'I DRUNG DU
GRUB RGYAL LUGS KYI TSE DBANG ZHUS,

DAM PA'I CHOS KYI BDUD RTZIR THOG MAR ROL, DGUNG LO BDUN BZHES
PA NA, KHRI CHEN BLO BZANG NYI

MA'I DRUNG DU RAB TU BYUNG, MING BLO BZANG BSTAN PA RAB RGYAS
BTAGS, DE NAS KLOG SLOB PA'I

MGO BTZUGS, LO DE'I ZLA BA BCU PA'I TSES GCIG NYIN PAR RANG
KHYIM NAS BTEGS TE, NYA 'BAN

RGYAL RI THANG SOGS BRGYUD NAS TSES LNGA NYIN PAR BLA MA GONG
MA'I GDAN SA BKRA SHIS BSHAD SGRUB GLING DU

'BYOR, DGE 'DUN PA RNAMS KYIS SER SGRENG GZAB RGYAS DANG BCAS
BSUS TE GDAN KHRIR BKOD,

DGUNG LO BRGYAD PAR, DRAN DBANG MKHAS BTZUN SENG GE'I ZHABS
DRUNG DU BZANG PO SPYOD PA'I SMON

LAM SOGS SBYOR KLOG DAG PAR BSLABS, BTZUN PA 'JAM DBYANGS SHES
RAB SLOB DPON DU BSKOS,

DGUNG LO DGU PAR SHUGS YAG RI KHROD DU PHEBS, YE SHES RGYA
MTSO'I SPYAN SNGAR DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA

MNOS, 'DUL BA'I BSLAB BYA RNAMS ZHIB KHRID DANG GUNG TSIGS SOGS
MA CHAG PAR BYAS, DGUNG

LO BCU PAR LHA 'BRUM BTAB, RJE GONG MA'I DNGOS SLOB SMAN PA DGE
LEGS KYIS CO NE MKHAN PO'I

MDUN NAS SMAN 'KHYER YONG BA BZHES PAS MYUR DU BDE BAR GROL,
KHONG GI 'BRUM KOG LA BRTEN NAS

BYIS PA BRGYA LHAG 'BRUM NAD LAS THAR, DGUNG LO BCU GCIG PAR
RANG YUL DU PHEBS, SER SKYA

MANG TSOGS RNAMS LA GRUB RGYAL LUGS KYI TSE DBANG BSKUR, SGROS
DAG CING GSAL LA LHAG CHAD MED

PAS, PHA KHU SOGS DGA' SPRO CHEN PO BSKYED, DGUNG LO BCU GNYIS
NAS BCO BRGYAD BAR LO

BDUN RING, DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN DU MAR BSTEN NAS DBANG LUNG
KHRID SOGS ZHUS SHING KHONG RANG

NYID NAS KYANG DBANG LUNG SOGS GNANG, DGUNG LO BCU DGU PAR DRIN
CHE BA'I YUM DUS KYI CHOS NYID

KHA'I NYER 'DABS G-YI DGE'I LUNG

PAR RTA PHYUG CES PA'I GRONG DU, YAB KHE BA CANG AE HAR DANG,
YUM LO ZA THAR MO MTSO GNYIS KYI

SRAS SU RAB BYUNG BCU GCIG PA'I CHU PHO RTA'I LO (1642) ZLA BA
BCU GCIG PA'I TSES BCU'I DGONG MO

MTSAN PHYED LA SKU BLTAMS, DGUNG GRANGS GSUM BZHIR PHEBS SKABS
DA DUNG SMRA MI SHES PA'I LKUG PA

LTA BUR GYUR, DE NAS YAB YUM GYIS GTZANG SBRA SOGS THABS SNA
TSOGS LA 'BAD CING DGE BSNYEN BSGRUB

BCUG PAS RIM GYIS SMRA SHES PAR GYUR, DE GAR BOD PA BLA RGAN
ZHES PA'I BLA MA ZHIG BZHUGS PA

DES, KHONG LA DGE 'DUN SKYABS ZHES PA'I MTSAN GSOL, DE NAS RING
PO MA LON PAR THANG RING

DGON GYI KHRI PA TSUL KHRIMS RGYA MTSOS YAB LA BU 'DIR KHRID
SHOG CES DGON PAR BOS, BLA MA GONG

MA GRAGS PA 'OD ZER GYI DNGOS CHAS RNAMS NGOS 'DZIN BYED
BCUG  DBUS LHA LDAN DU BZHUGS YOD

PA'I BLA MA GONG MA'I DBON PO BLO GROS 'OD ZER MDUN, BYIS PA'I
GNAS TSUL SOGS KYI 'PHRIN YIG

PHUL, BLO GROS 'OD ZER GYIS PAn CHEN BLO BZANG CHOS KYI RGYAL
MTSAN LA GNAS TSUL SNYAN ZHU PHUL BAS,

PAn CHEN NAS GRAGS PA 'OD ZER GYI SKU SKYE RU NGOS 'DZIN MDZAD
DE, RE ZHIG THANG RING DGON DU ZHOG

CES PA'I BKA' GNANG, DE NAS THANG RING DGON DU SONG NAS, DGON
DE'I KHRI ZUR TSUL KHRIMS RGYA

MTSO DANG, KHRI PA PHUN TSOGS BZANG PO GNYIS KYI SPYAN SNGAR
GTZUG PHUD PHUL TE RAB TU BYUNG, MING

BSTAN 'DZIN LEGS BSHAD RGYA MTSOR BTAGS, SBYOR KLOG DANG BLOR
'DZIN GYI DBU TSUGS,

DGUNG GRANGS DGU PAR DGON LUNG DGA' LDAN BYAMS PA GLING DU
PHEBS, MCHOD YON KUN GYIS BRTZI

'JOG CHEN PO BYAS, DGUNG LO BCU GCIG PAR, TZONG KHA'I STOD SKAR
MA'I THANG CHEN DU, LNGA PA

CHEN PO PE CING DU PHEBS PA MJAL BAR PHYIN, DGUNG LO NYI SHUR
PHEBS PA LCAGS MO GLANG GI LOR

DBUS LHA LDAN DU PHEBS, LNGA PA CHEN PO MJAL ZHING KHONG GI
SPYAN SNGAR DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA MNOS,

BLO BZANG CHOS LDAN ZHES PA'I MING GNANG, DE NAS DGON KHAG DANG

PA BLANGS, DGUNG LO NYER BDUN

CHEN MOR GRVA SKOR MDZAD, DGUNG LO

MKHAN MO BLO BZANG PADMA LA TZONG KHA PA DANG, PAn CHEN GONG

MDO SNGAGS KYI GZHUNG RNAMS LA

ZHE GNYIS PA CHU MO PHAG GI LOR,

DU TSUR PHEBS, DGON

LUNG RI KHROD BYANG CHUB GLING DU BZHUGS, PHYI LOR THANG RING
DGON DANG SKU 'BUM SOGS SU PHEBS,

DGUNG LO ZHE DRUG PAR, LO GSAR SMON LAM CHEN PO 'TSOGS PA DANG,
GONG MA MJAL BA'I CHED

GNANG, LAN GNYIS PAR GONG MA CHEN

CHEN PO MDZAD CING MGUL DAR

CING BSDAD MI DGOS PA'I

DGONGS PA NAN TAN GYIS ZHUS NAS KHROL, DGUNG LO NGA GNYIS PA CHU
MO BYA'I LOR GONG MAS DRUNG DU

GYIS LAM DU ZHUGS, PE CING

KYI SBYIN PA RGYA CHER BSTZAL, DGUNG

RTZOM PA PO'I LO RGYUS NYUNG BSDUS,...

*, LCANG SKYA ROL PA'I RDO RJE'AM YE SHES BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME NI
MDO SMAD TZONG KHA BYANG GI PHYOGS

SU RGYA BOD 'DRES MAR BSDAD PA'I SA CHA LANG GRU'U ZHES PA'I
'BROG SDER, HOR GYI RUS SU GTOGS

PA'I YAB CHI GYA TSANGS PA GU RU BSTAN 'DZIN DANG, YUM BU SKYID
GNYIS KYI SRAS SU, RAB BYUNG

BCU GNYIS PA'I ME MO BYA'I LO (1717) ZLA BA DANG PO'I TSES BCU
NYIN SKU BLTAMS, DGUNG LO BZHI

PAR PHEBS PA NA, 'JAM BZHAD 'JIGS MED DBANG POS LCANG SKYA BLO
BZANG CHOS LDAN GYI SPRUL SKUR

NGOS 'DZIN MDZAD, SKABS DER SOG PO'I WANG STOBS CHEN ZHIG GI BU
LCANG SKYA'I SPRUL SKU YIN PAR

BSGRAGS STABS, RE ZHIG BAR GONG MAR ZHU RGYU 'GYANGS DGOS
THUG  DE NAS THU'U BKVAN CHOS KYI RGYA

MTSOS THUGS KHUR BZHES TE GONG MAR ZHUS PAS, GDAN SAR GDAN
DRONGS ZHES PA'I BKA' THOB,

PE CING NAS DKA' CHEN SHES RAB DAR RGYAS DANG DEM CHI BCAS,
LCAGS BYI ZLA BA LNGA PAR LANG GRU'U LA

SPRUL SKU GDAN 'DREN DU 'BYOR, TSES GCIG NYIN PAR GZIM GUR DU
GDAN DRANGS NAS GSOL STON

RGYA CHEN PHUL ZHING, GONG MAS GNANG BA'I DNGOS 'BUL SPAM MTHO
BA PHUL, TSES GSUM NYIN PAR

DGON LUNG PHYOGS SU CHIBS KHA BSGYUR, TSES PA BCU'I NYIN BLA
DPON SER SKYA STONG PHRAG MANG POS

BSU BA DANG BCAS LCANG SKYA BLA BRANG DU 'BYOR, LCANG SKYA GONG
MA'I SLOB MA AA RTZE CHOS RJE BLO BZANG CHOS

'DZIN MDUN NAS 'BRI KLOG SBYOR SDEB SOGS SBYONG BA'I MGO BTZUGS,
DGUNG LO BDUN PAR BLO BZANG

BSTAN PA'I RGYAL MTSAN MDUN NAS DGE BSNYEN GYI SDOM PA BLANGS,
RAB BYUNG BCU GNYIS PA'I CHU MO

YOS KYI LO (1723) LA MTSO SNGON GYI DPON BSTAN 'DZIN CHING WANG
SOGS NAS GONG MAR RGOL PA'I DUS

ZING BSLANGS, CANG JUN GUNG NYEN G-YO'U DANG, GUNG YO'U GRUNG
CHI GNYIS KYIS DPUNG CHEN BTEGS

NAS MTSO SOG CHAM LA PHAB, DGON SDE MANG POR GONG MA'I BKA' CHAD
PHOG  SHING PHO 'BRUG GI LO

@497

(1724) LA DGON LUNG DGON PA SHUL MED DU BRLAGS, LCANG SKYA SPRUL
SKU DGON LUNG NAS NYIN LAM

GNYIS TZAM GYI SAR MCHOD RTEN THANG DGON PA'I NYE 'DABS NAGS
TSAL STUG POR BRAG PHUG CIG TU GAB

NAS BZHUGS, SKABS DER GONG MA YUNG TRING RGYAL SAR PHEBS NAS LO
GNYIS PA YIN ZHING, LCANG

SKYA GONG MAR ZAB CHOS ZHUS MYONG BAS THUGS DAD KHYAD PAR CAN
YOD STABS, SPRUL SKUR BAR CHAD 'BYUNG

DOGS KYIS DE 'PHRAL CANG JUN GNYIS LA PE CING DU GDAN DRANG DGOS
PA'I BKA' PHAB, CANG JUN

GNYIS KYIS THABS SNA TSOGS LA BRTEN TE NAGS TSAL NAS ZI LING DU
GDAN DRANGS, DE NAS RGYA NAG TU

PHEBS, GONG MAS KHONG ZUNG GRU ZI DGON PAR LCANG SKYA GONG MA'I
GDAN SAR BKOD, DKA' CHEN

SHES RAB DAR RGYAS SLOB DPON DU BRTEN NAS, MDO SNGAGS KYI GZHUNG
CHEN RNAMS LA GSAN SBYONG MDZAD,

DGUNG LO BCO BRGYAD PA'I DUS SU RIG GNAS KUN LA MKHAS PAR GYUR,
RGYA DANG SOG PO MAN JU BCAS

KYI SKAD YIG KYANG KHONG DU CHUD, SKABS DER GONG MAS ``BYAMS ?
BRTZES 'GRO BA YONGS KYI SPYI BO NAS

DBANG BSKUR BA'I KUN MKHYEN BLA MA'' ? ZHES PA'I MTSAN SNYAN
DANG GSER SRANG BRGYAD CU LAS GRUB PA'I THAM

KA  GSER YIG BCAS GNANG NAS CHAB SRID CHEN PO'I BLA MAR BKUR,
SHING PHO STAG GI LO (1734)

LA GONG MA'I BKA' BZHIN, RGYAL SRAS BCU BDUN PA KHENG ZI CHING
WANG DANG LHAN CIG  T'A LA'I

DBUS SU GDAN DRANGS NAS PO TA LA'I GDAN SAR 'GOD PA'I CHED DU
KHAMS PHYOGS SU PHEBS, ZLA BA

BCU GCIG PA'I TSES NYER GSUM NYIN MGAR THAR DU 'BYOR, T'A LA'I
MDUN PAR GONG MAS GNANG BA'I

GSER YIG BSGRAGS SHING DNGOS 'BUL RGYA CHEN PHUL, DGUNG LO BCU
DGU PA SHING MO YOS KYI LO'I

(1735) ZLA BA GSUM PAR KHAMS LHO BRGYUD KYI NYAG CHU RDZONG DANG
LI THANG SOGS BRGYUD DE DBUS SU

PHEBS, ZLA BA BDUN PA'I TSES BCU BDUN NYIN PAR T'A LA'I PO TA
LAR GDAN KHRIR BKOD, ZLA BA

BCU PAR GTZANG DU PHEBS, TSES BRGYAD LA BKRA SHIS LHUN POR
'BYOR, TSES DGU NYIN PAR PAn

CHEN BLO BZANG YE SHES MJAL KHA ZHUS, ZLA BA BCU PA'I TSES BCU
GSUM NYIN PAn CHEN LAS RAB BYUNG

DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA MNOS, MTSAN YE SHES BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME
ZHES PA GNANG, TSES BCU BDUN NYIN

PAn CHEN MDUN NAS DGE SLONG GI SDOM PA MNOS, SKABS DER GONG MA
YUNG TRING GNAM DU GSHEGS

PA'I GNAS TSUL 'BYOR BAS, 'PHRAL DU DBUS SU PHYIR PHEBS, 'BRUG
LOR RGYA NAG TU CHIBS KHA

BSGYUR, DAR MDO SOGS BRGYUD DE PE CING DU PHEBS, GONG MA CHAN
LUNG NAS KHONG PE CING GI THAM

KA BLA MAR BSKOS, DGUNG LO NYER LNGAR PHEBS PA LCAGS MO BYA'I
LOR GONG MAS BSTAN 'GYUR SOG

YIG TU BSGYUR DGOS PA'I BKA' PHEBS, ZLA BA BCU PAR DBU BTZUGS,
LO TZ'A BA MANG PO DANG

LHAN CIG CHU PHO KHYI'I LO ZLA BA BCU GCIG PA'I TSES BCO LNGA
NYIN PAR MJUG GRUB PAR MDZAD, PHYIS SU

PE CING DU DPAR BTAB NAS SOG YUL KUN TU KHYAB BO, DGUNG LO SO
GSUM DU PHEBS PA SA MO SBRUL

@498

KYI LOR GONG MAR DGONGS PA ZHUS TE MDO SMAD RANG YUL DU PHEBS,
T'A LA'I YON TAN RGYA MTSOS BTAB

PA'I DGON LUNG DU, KHRI ZUR SUM PA ZHABS DRUNG SOGS CHE DGUS SER
SBRENG DANG BCAS BSUS,

DE NAS SKU 'BUM DGON SOGS SU PHEBS NAS DAM CHOS BSTZAL, ZLA BA
BRGYAD PAR PE CING DU TSUR

PHEBS, KHONG DGUNG LO ZHE GCIG TU PHEBS PA RAB BYUNG BCU GSUM
PA'I ME MO GLANG GI LO (1757)

ZLA BA GNYIS PA'I TSES GSUM NYIN PAR, T'A LA'I BDUN PA DGONGS PA
RDZOGS PA'I GNAS TSUL PE CING

DU 'BYOR, GONG MAS BKA' PHEBS LTAR, T'A LA'I SKYE PHRENG NGOS
'DZIN PA'I CHAD DU, AAM PAN GCIG

DANG GONG MA'I BLA SMAN PA GNYIS, DPON CHUNG KHA SHAS DANG BCAS
KHAMS DAR RTZE MDO SOGS BRGYUD

DE DBUS SU PHEBS, ZLA BA BCU GNYIS PAR LHA SAR 'BYOR, PHYI LO'I
ZLA BA BZHI PAR GTZANG BKRA SHIS

LHUN POR BSKYOD, PAn CHEN BLO BZANG DPAL LDAN YE SHES DANG ZHAL
'DZOMS, SNAR THANG DU CHOS MJAL

PHEBS RJES DBUS SU PHYIR PHEBS, LCAGS PHO 'BRUG GI LOR PE CING
DU PHYIR PHEBS, SKABS DER GONG

MA'I PHO BRANG DU LCANG SKYA MA GTOGS BLA CHEN GZHAN MED PAR
BRTEN, GONG MAS THU'U BKVAN CHOS KYI NYI

MA PE CING YONG DGOS PA'I BKA' PHEBS, DE NAS THU'U BKVAN RGYA
NAG TU PHEBS NAS KHONG GI SLOB MAR

GYUR, DGUNG GRANGS NGA GCIG BZHES PA ME PHAG LO NAS BZUNG DBYAR
KHAR ZLA BA BZHI PA NAS BRGYAD

PA'I BAR RI BO RTZE LNGAR BZHUGS SHING, DER AE WAm DGA' 'KHYIL
ZHES PA'I SGRUB KHANG ZHIG KYANG BTAB,

DGUNG LO NGA LNGAR PHEBS PA LCAGS MO YOS KYI LOR GONG MAS BKA'
PHEBS LTAR, RGYAL BA'I BKA'

'GYUR RO COG MAN JU'I SKAD YIG TU BSGYUR BAR MDZAD, PE CING GI
BLA MA MKHAS PA DANG, HVA

SHANG YON TAN BZANG BA RNAMS LA SGYUR BCUG  BLA MA RANG GIS ZHUS
PAR MA TSAD GONG MAS KYANG ZHU

PA'I ME PHO RTA'I LO

CHED DMIGS KYIS PE CING DU SONG NAS

GONG MAR GNAS TSUL ZHUS, GONG MAS 'PHRAL DU CHOG BKA' GNANG BAR

GONG MA'I GDAN KHRIR BZHUGS,

DGUNG GRANGS BCU GCIG TU PHEBS PA LCAGS BYI LO'I ZLA BA DRUG
PAR, PAn CHEN RIN PO CHE PE CING

DU PHEBS LAM SOG YUL BRGYUD PA MJAL ZHING DAM CHOS ZHUS PA DANG
DNGOS 'BUL RGYA CHEN BSTABS,

NGAG DBANG DPAL 'BYOR 'DAS, DE

LO'I ZLA BA BDUN PA'I TSES BCU

RJE MJAL, 'JIGS BYED LHA BCU GSUM

PA'I RDO RJE RTING MA'I MJAL KHA

MIN DVANG BAR GYUR, LO DE'I

DBANG TSUL KHRIMS PE CING DU GDAN
